\doxysubsubsection{LSM6\+DSO32 }
\hypertarget{group___l_s_m6_d_s_o32}{}\label{group___l_s_m6_d_s_o32}\index{LSM6DSO32@{LSM6DSO32}}


This file provides a set of functions needed to drive the lsm6dso32 enhanced inertial module.

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Sensor hub source register.\+[get]\+. \end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\doxysubsubsubsection{Detailed Description}
This file provides a set of functions needed to drive the lsm6dso32 enhanced inertial module. 

This section groups all the functions concerning main serial interface management (not auxiliary).

\label{doc-func-members}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group___l_s_m6_d_s_o32_gab494eb8e9e05c91a7a1df20c6d2b6630} 
int32\+\_\+t lsm6dso32\+\_\+tap\+\_\+dur\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structstmdev__ctx__t}{stmdev\+\_\+ctx\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ctx}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



When double tap recognition is enabled, this register expresses the maximum time between two consecutive detected taps to determine a double tap event. The default value of these bits is 0000b which corresponds to 16\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+ODR\+\_\+\+XL time. If the DUR\+[3:\+0]\+ bits are set to a different value, 1LSB corresponds to 32\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+ODR\+\_\+\+XL time.\+[get]\+.

int32\+\_\+t lsm6dso32\+\_\+tap\+\_\+quiet\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structstmdev__ctx__t}{stmdev\+\_\+ctx\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ctx}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Quiet time is the time after the first detected tap in which there must not be any over threshold event. The default value of these bits is 00b which corresponds to 2\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+ODR\+\_\+\+XL time. If the QUIET\+[1:\+0]\+ bits are set to a different value, 1LSB corresponds to 4\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+ODR\+\_\+\+XL time.\+[get]\+.
